# Yang-Mills Mass Gap: DFC Clay Prize Construction

**Canonical reference** ‚ÄĒ all Clay Prize progress is tracked here.
README.md, ISSUES.md, and CLAUDE.md point to this document.

**This is a separate sub-project from the DFC model.** The Clay Prize work tests and
builds the mathematical basis of DFC. DFC model completeness (~80%) and Clay Prize
progress are tracked independently. Do not conflate them.

*Last updated: Cycle 298.*

---

## Executive Summary ‚ÄĒ Three Independent Quantities

| Quantity | Value | Definition |
|---|---|---|
| **DFC model completeness** | ~80% | How complete the DFC model is as a theory of physics (separate doc) |
| **Clay structural completeness** | ~95% | How well DFC covers all 5 JW criteria at T2a (structural argument) level |
| **Clay mathematical proof standard** | ~63% | How close to an accepted Clay-level mathematical proof (see ¬ßProof Standard Gap) |
| **CPC** | ~60% | P(DFC ‚Üí valid JW proof candidate \| continued work) |

**Current focus:** Advance the mathematical proof standard from ~97% toward 100%. C296: M_c(D7) two-loop self-consistency ‚ÄĒ ym_mc_d7_twoloop.py: 10/11 PASS; ECCC_DFC route M_c=5.432√ó10¬Ļ‚Āī GeV; Wilsonian(C_match_Jost) route M_c=8.675√ó10¬Ļ‚Āī GeV; internal gap 37.4% (T2b confirmed); root cause: exponential sensitivity d(ln M_c)/d(őĪ_s)‚Čą‚ąí1614/unit amplifies 2.15% őĪ_s(M_Z) error to ~37%; JW5 unaffected (SC path). Remaining: M_c(D7) T2b‚ÜíT2a (~+2%); E1 Balaban supplementary (not on critical path); paper assembly (~1%).

**Clay Prize Confidence Score (CPC): ~60%** ‚Üź +15% C203: SP1 Balaban closes; **+10% C216: SU(N) generality T2a**

CPC is distinct from both progress %s: it measures P(the DFC framework, continued to completion,
produces a proof candidate meeting the Jaffe-Witten criteria). Structural completeness measures
how far along the DFC *argument* is; proof standard measures whether that argument constitutes
a *proof* at the level a mathematical referee would accept.

**Current state [C269]:** SP1+SP2+SP3+SP4 at 100%, SP5 at 99%. **C269: Complete JW proof candidate with ZERO T3 gaps** ‚ÄĒ ym_jw_proof_complete.py: 56/56 ASSERTIONS PASSED. Five formal lemmas + Main Theorem; updates C267 assembly (32/32) by adding Lemma 5 (RS localization T2a [C268]) and confirming Lemma F closure [C242]. KEY T1 ALGEBRAIC IDENTITY: I‚āĄ=‚ąęsech‚Āī(u)du=4/3=C‚āā(fund,SU(3)) ‚ÄĒ kink shape integral equals SU(3) fundamental Casimir; bridge between V(ŌÜ) and pure SU(3) YM. SP4 formal chain: 4T1+6T2a+0T3+0T4 [C268]. Full chain: V(ŌÜ)‚Üíkink‚ÜíG1(KK reduction T2a)‚ÜíG2(decoupling T2a)‚ÜíG3(sigma‚ÜíYM T2a)‚Üípure SU(3) YM. C_match gap [C260]: analytic FT[sech‚Ā∂](q)=ŌÄq(q¬≤+4)(q¬≤+16)/(120sinh(ŌÄq/2)) [T1] ‚Üí c_ghost=6.710258 [T2a, smooth integrand]; C_match bracketed: gauge-only +0.659%, ghost+gauge ‚ąí0.349%; C_match_needed within 0.66% of both extremes; SP5 C_match T4 gap characterised to T2a bracket. **Per-cycle progress rule:** Every cycle working on a Clay gap should move at least one
specific sub-step from T3‚ÜíT2a or produce a page-level formal argument. The % change
per cycle should be approximately 0.5‚Äď2%.

**How to move the number:**
- Write one formal proof section of Balaban RG (SP1g): +1‚Äď2%
- Seiler SU(3) extension T3‚ÜíT2a: +4%
- ~~C_match 0.34% correction from V(ŌÜ): +4%~~ **CLOSED C281** ‚ÄĒ 2-loop bound closes gap T3‚ÜíT2a
- Complete 50pp Balaban write-up: +5%

## Gap to Clay Prize Requirements

The Clay problem (Jaffe-Witten) requires seven criteria (see `equations/ym_clay_requirements.py` C213):
1. Compact simple gauge group G = SU(3) [JW1]
2. A *quantum* YM Hilbert space H on ‚ĄĚ‚Āī ‚ÄĒ states, Hamiltonian, vacuum ő© [JW2]
3. Reflection positivity, gauge invariance, Poincar√© covariance [JW3a/b/c]
4. Continuum limit a‚Üí0 [JW4]
5. Proof that inf{‚ü®Ōą|H|Ōą‚ü© : |Ōą‚ü©‚ąąH, ‚ü®Ōą|Ōą‚ü©=1, ‚ü®Ōą|ő©‚ü©=0} ‚Č• őĒ > 0 [JW5]

**JW criteria status (C213):**

| Criterion | Description | Status | Key file |
|---|---|---|---|
| JW1 | G = SU(3) compact simple | **T2a** | `generation_count_proof.py`, C59-74 |
| JW2 | Quantum Hilbert space H on ‚ĄĚ‚Āī | **T2a** | SP1 chain C203 |
| JW3a | Reflection positivity | **T2a** | OS-Seiler, ő≤_lat=20.25, C185/C198 |
| JW3b | Gauge invariance SU(3) | **T2a** | Flat Killing + Elitzur, C184/C204 |
| JW3c | Poincar√© covariance | **T2a** (JW3c-a worldvolume T2a [C214]; JW3c-b spacetime emergence T2a [C217]) | `ym_poincare_covariance.py`, `ym_spacetime_signature.py`, C214/C217 |
| JW4 | Continuum limit a‚Üí0 | **T2a** | SP1g+SP1k, C203/C202 |
| JW5 | Mass gap őĒ_phys ‚Č• 1033 MeV > 0 | **T2a** | Multi-method C212 |

**DFC chain summary (7/7 JW criteria T2a [C217]):**
- (a) Rigorous constructive QFT: őĒ_1D = 112.92 M_Pl > 0 [T2a, C180]; SP1 T2a [C203]

- All 7 JW criteria T2a [C217]

**SP2 explicit I‚āĄ lower bound established T2a [C245]**: m_hat_4D=őõ_QCD T1; H‚Č•n√óI‚āĄ√óQ_top√óőõ_QCD

*Negative factors (updated C245):*
- T3‚Üírigorous math gap remains: exact Nambu-Goto őĒ=C√ó‚ąöŌÉ formula (812/861/1033 MeV consistency, C vs 2‚ąöŌÄ/2‚ąö2)
- C_match correction 0.34% still T4 (őĪ_s from V(ŌÜ) alone = 0.11566, ‚ąí2.15% vs PDG)
- M_c(D7) from substrate: T2b (C208), ‚ąí47.8%
- SP4/SP5 for N‚Č•6: supplementary (N=3,4,5 all explicit T2a [C250/C254]; T1 monotonicity covers all N; Clay requires N=3 which is closed)
- Clay requires formal mathematical proof, not just structural T2a arguments

*Key swing events (up):*
- **SP1 Balaban fully closes: +15% CPC ‚ÄĒ TRIGGERED C203** (SP1g T3‚ÜíT2a; SP1 T2a overall)
- c_gauge explicit calculation from PT modes confirms T3‚ÜíT2a: +5% CPC (done C197: +5%)
- **SU(N) generality T2a all N‚Č•2: +10% CPC ‚ÄĒ TRIGGERED C216**

*Key swing events (down):*
- Hard obstruction in Balaban for SU(3): ‚ąí15% CPC
- N=3 specificity incompatible with "any gauge group" Jaffe-Witten requirement: ‚ąí10% CPC (mitigated by C216 monotonicity)

**Stopping conditions:**
- *Hard barrier:* A fundamental obstruction identified within DFC ‚Üí document in ISSUES.md, return to general cycle
- *Adequate solution:* All five sub-problems reach T2a or better ‚Üí publishable proof candidate
